        double node_1771288499763_chaosThreshold = inp_entropy_chaosThreshold_1288499763;
        double node_1771288499763_transitionThreshold = inp_entropy_transitionThres_1288499763;
        
        // Buffer para entropía sin suavizar (estático para persistencia)
        static double node_1771288499763_rawBuffer[];
        static int node_1771288499763_bufferSize = 0;
        
        // Inicializar buffer si es necesario
        if (node_1771288499763_bufferSize < node_1771288499763_smooth) {
            ArrayResize(node_1771288499763_rawBuffer, node_1771288499763_smooth);
            ArrayInitialize(node_1771288499763_rawBuffer, 0.0);
            node_1771288499763_bufferSize = node_1771288499763_smooth;
        }
        
        // Verificar que hay suficientes datos
        int node_1771288499763_totalBars = iBars(_Symbol, _Period);
        if (node_1771288499763_totalBars >= node_1771288499763_period + node_1771288499763_smooth + 1) {
            
            double node_1771288499763_max_val = -DBL_MAX;
            double node_1771288499763_min_val = DBL_MAX;
            
            // Buffer temporal para retornos logarítmicos
            double node_1771288499763_returns[];
            ArrayResize(node_1771288499763_returns, node_1771288499763_period);
            
            // 1. Calcular Retornos Logarítmicos
            for (int node_1771288499763_k = 0; node_1771288499763_k < node_1771288499763_period; node_1771288499763_k++) {
                double node_1771288499763_current_price = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, node_1771288499763_k);
                double node_1771288499763_prev_price = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, node_1771288499763_k + 1);
                
                double node_1771288499763_log_return = 0.0;
                if (node_1771288499763_prev_price > 0) {
                    node_1771288499763_log_return = MathLog(node_1771288499763_current_price / node_1771288499763_prev_price);
                }
                
                node_1771288499763_returns[node_1771288499763_k] = node_1771288499763_log_return;
                
                if (node_1771288499763_log_return > node_1771288499763_max_val) node_1771288499763_max_val = node_1771288499763_log_return;
                if (node_1771288499763_log_return < node_1771288499763_min_val) node_1771288499763_min_val = node_1771288499763_log_return;
            }
            
            double node_1771288499763_range = node_1771288499763_max_val - node_1771288499763_min_val;
            double node_1771288499763_normalized_entropy = 0.0;
            
            // Si hay rango (mercado moviéndose), calculamos entropía
            if (node_1771288499763_range > 0) {
                
                // 2. Discretización en bins
                int node_1771288499763_bin_counts[];
                ArrayResize(node_1771288499763_bin_counts, node_1771288499763_bins);
                ArrayInitialize(node_1771288499763_bin_counts, 0);
                
                double node_1771288499763_bin_size = node_1771288499763_range / node_1771288499763_bins;
                if (node_1771288499763_bin_size == 0) node_1771288499763_bin_size = 0.0000001;
                
                for (int node_1771288499763_k2 = 0; node_1771288499763_k2 < node_1771288499763_period; node_1771288499763_k2++) {
                    double node_1771288499763_val = node_1771288499763_returns[node_1771288499763_k2];
                    int node_1771288499763_bin_index = (int)((node_1771288499763_val - node_1771288499763_min_val) / node_1771288499763_bin_size);
                    if (node_1771288499763_bin_index >= node_1771288499763_bins) node_1771288499763_bin_index = node_1771288499763_bins - 1;
                    if (node_1771288499763_bin_index < 0) node_1771288499763_bin_index = 0;
                    node_1771288499763_bin_counts[node_1771288499763_bin_index]++;
                }
                
                // 3. Calcular Shannon Entropy
                double node_1771288499763_entropy = 0.0;
                for (int node_1771288499763_j = 0; node_1771288499763_j < node_1771288499763_bins; node_1771288499763_j++) {
                    if (node_1771288499763_bin_counts[node_1771288499763_j] > 0) {
                        double node_1771288499763_p = (double)node_1771288499763_bin_counts[node_1771288499763_j] / node_1771288499763_period;
                        node_1771288499763_entropy -= node_1771288499763_p * MathLog(node_1771288499763_p) / MathLog(2.0);
                    }
                }
                
                // 4. Normalización
                double node_1771288499763_max_possible_entropy = MathLog(node_1771288499763_bins) / MathLog(2.0);
                if (node_1771288499763_max_possible_entropy > 0) {
                    node_1771288499763_normalized_entropy = node_1771288499763_entropy / node_1771288499763_max_possible_entropy;
                }
            }
            
            // 5. Aplicar Sensibilidad (Contraste)
            double node_1771288499763_processed_entropy = MathPow(node_1771288499763_normalized_entropy, node_1771288499763_sensitivity);
            
            // Desplazar buffer hacia atrás e insertar nuevo valor
            for (int node_1771288499763_s = node_1771288499763_smooth - 1; node_1771288499763_s > 0; node_1771288499763_s--) {
                node_1771288499763_rawBuffer[node_1771288499763_s] = node_1771288499763_rawBuffer[node_1771288499763_s - 1];
            }
            node_1771288499763_rawBuffer[0] = node_1771288499763_processed_entropy;
            
            // 6. Suavizado (SMA simple)
            double node_1771288499763_sum = 0.0;
            for (int node_1771288499763_ss = 0; node_1771288499763_ss < node_1771288499763_smooth; node_1771288499763_ss++) {
                node_1771288499763_sum += node_1771288499763_rawBuffer[node_1771288499763_ss];
            }
            node_1771288499763_value = node_1771288499763_sum / node_1771288499763_smooth;
            
            // Determinar zona basada en umbrales
            if (node_1771288499763_value >= node_1771288499763_chaosThreshold) {
                node_1771288499763_chaos = true;
                node_1771288499763_transition = false;
                node_1771288499763_flow = false;
            } else if (node_1771288499763_value >= node_1771288499763_transitionThreshold) {
                node_1771288499763_chaos = false;
                node_1771288499763_transition = true;
                node_1771288499763_flow = false;
            } else {
                node_1771288499763_chaos = false;
                node_1771288499763_transition = false;
                node_1771288499763_flow = true;
            }
        }
        
        LogDebug("ENTROPY [node_1771288499763]: Value=" + DoubleToString(node_1771288499763_value, 4) + 
                 " Chaos=" + (node_1771288499763_chaos ? "YES" : "NO") +
                 " Transition=" + (node_1771288499763_transition ? "YES" : "NO") +
                 " Flow=" + (node_1771288499763_flow ? "YES" : "NO"));

    // Node: logic.threshold (ID: node_1771288478585)

        // Threshold Logic (MQL5)
        double node_1771288478585_value = node_1771288499763_value;
        bool node_1771288478585_result = (node_1771288478585_value < inp_threshol_threshold_1288478585);

    // Node: logic.threshold (ID: node_1772468523032)

        // Threshold Logic (MQL5)
        double node_1772468523032_value = node_1771288439472_value;
        bool node_1772468523032_result = (node_1772468523032_value < inp_threshol_threshold_2468523032);

    // Node: logic.or (ID: node_1772468550390)

        // OR Logic (MQL5) - 2 conditions
        bool node_1772468550390_result = ((node_1771288471877_result) || (node_1772468523032_result));

    // Node: math.constant (ID: node_1772475000701)
    double node_1772475000701_result = inp_constant_value_2475000701;

    // Node: logic.threshold (ID: node_1772475005277)

        // Threshold Logic (MQL5)
        double node_1772475005277_value = node_1772475000701_result;
        bool node_1772475005277_result = (node_1772475005277_value > inp_threshol_threshold_2475005277);

    // Node: logic.not (ID: node_1772475070515)

        // NOT Logic (MQL5)
        bool node_1772475070515_result = !(node_1772475005277_result);

    // Node: indicator.ma (ID: node_1772474855530)

        // Moving Average (MQL5)
        double node_1772474855530_value = GetMA(inp_ma_period_2474855530, inp_ma_shift_2474855530, (ENUM_MA_METHOD)inp_ma_maType_2474855530, PRICE_CLOSE, 0);
        double node_1772474855530_prev = GetMA(inp_ma_period_2474855530, inp_ma_shift_2474855530, (ENUM_MA_METHOD)inp_ma_maType_2474855530, PRICE_CLOSE, 1);

    // Node: indicator.ma (ID: node_1772474888650)

        // Moving Average (MQL5)
        double node_1772474888650_value = GetMA(inp_ma_period_2474888650, inp_ma_shift_2474888650, (ENUM_MA_METHOD)inp_ma_maType_2474888650, PRICE_CLOSE, 0);
        double node_1772474888650_prev = GetMA(inp_ma_period_2474888650, inp_ma_shift_2474888650, (ENUM_MA_METHOD)inp_ma_maType_2474888650, PRICE_CLOSE, 1);

    // Node: logic.comparison (ID: node_1772474944515)

        // Comparison Logic (MQL5)
        double node_1772474944515_value1 = node_1772474855530_value;
        double node_1772474944515_value2 = node_1772474888650_value;
        bool node_1772474944515_result = (node_1772474944515_value1 > node_1772474944515_value2);

    // Node: logic.and (ID: node_1772475059750)

        // AND Logic (MQL5) - 2 conditions
        bool node_1772475059750_result = ((node_1772475005277_result) && (node_1772474944515_result));

    // Node: logic.or (ID: node_1772475075476)

        // OR Logic (MQL5) - 2 conditions
        bool node_1772475075476_result = ((node_1772475059750_result) || (node_1772475070515_result));

    // Node: math.constant (ID: node_1772478791296)
    double node_1772478791296_result = inp_constant_value_2478791296;

    // Node: logic.threshold (ID: node_1772478806075)

        // Threshold Logic (MQL5)
        double node_1772478806075_value = node_1772478791296_result;
        bool node_1772478806075_result = (node_1772478806075_value > inp_threshol_threshold_2478806075);

    // Node: logic.timeFilter (ID: node_1772478826124)

        // Time Filter Logic (MQL5) with GMT Offset
        bool node_1772478826124_result = false;
        {
            MqlDateTime timeStruct;
            TimeToStruct(TimeCurrent(), timeStruct);
            int serverHour = timeStruct.hour;
            int hour = serverHour + inp_timeFilt_gmtOffset_2478826124;
            
            // Handle hour wraparound
            if (hour < 0) hour += 24;
            if (hour >= 24) hour -= 24;
            
            int dayOfWeek = timeStruct.day_of_week;
            
            // Debug logging
            static datetime lastLogTime = 0;
            if (TimeCurrent() - lastLogTime >= 60) {
                lastLogTime = TimeCurrent();
                Print("TimeFilter: ServerHour=", serverHour, " Offset=inp_timeFilt_gmtOffset_2478826124", " AdjustedHour=", hour, " Range=inp_timeFilt_startHour_2478826124-inp_timeFilt_endHour_2478826124");
            }
            
            if ("HOUR_RANGE" == "HOUR_RANGE") {
                if (inp_timeFilt_startHour_2478826124 < inp_timeFilt_endHour_2478826124) {
                    node_1772478826124_result = (hour >= inp_timeFilt_startHour_2478826124 && hour < inp_timeFilt_endHour_2478826124);
                } else {
                    // Handle overnight ranges

                LogDebug("Crossunder node_1772665448360: New bar - prev1=" + DoubleToString(node_1772665448360_prevValue1, 5) + " prev2=" + DoubleToString(node_1772665448360_prevValue2, 5));
            }
            
            // Detect crossunder: curr1 < curr2 AND prev1 >= prev2
            node_1772665448360_result = (node_1772665448360_value1 < node_1772665448360_value2) && (node_1772665448360_prevValue1 >= node_1772665448360_prevValue2);
            
            if (node_1772665448360_result) {
                LogInfo("CROSSUNDER node_1772665448360 TRIGGERED! curr1=" + DoubleToString(node_1772665448360_value1, 5) + " < curr2=" + DoubleToString(node_1772665448360_value2, 5));
            }
        }
        
        // ALWAYS update lastTickValue at end of every tick
        node_1772665448360_lastTickValue1 = node_1772665448360_value1;
        node_1772665448360_lastTickValue2 = node_1772665448360_value2;
        
        // Confirmation bars check (runtime)
        static int node_1772665448360_confirmCount = 0;
        if (inp_crossund_confirmationBar_2665448360 > 0) {
            if (g_NewBar) {
                if (node_1772665448360_result) {
                    node_1772665448360_confirmCount++;
                } else {
                    node_1772665448360_confirmCount = 0;
                }
            }
            node_1772665448360_result = (node_1772665448360_confirmCount >= inp_crossund_confirmationBar_2665448360);
        }


    // Node: logic.and (ID: node_1772732162308)

        // AND Logic (MQL5) - 2 conditions
        bool node_1772732162308_result = ((node_1772665425680_result) && (node_1772665448360_result));

    // Node: indicator.currentPrice (ID: node_1772731284842)

        // Current Price - Low (MQL5)
        double node_1772731284842_value = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, inp_currentP_shift_2731284842);

    // Node: logic.crossunder (ID: node_1772804484172)

        // Crossunder Logic (MQL5) - FIX v2: Use lastTickValue to capture bar close correctly
        static double node_1772804484172_prevValue1 = 0;
        static double node_1772804484172_prevValue2 = 0;
        static double node_1772804484172_lastTickValue1 = 0;  // Value from previous tick
        static double node_1772804484172_lastTickValue2 = 0;  // Value from previous tick
        static datetime node_1772804484172_lastBarTime = 0;
        
        double node_1772804484172_value1 = node_1772731284842_value;
        double node_1772804484172_value2 = node_1772722416840_support_level;
        bool node_1772804484172_result = false;
        datetime node_1772804484172_currentBarTime = GetBarTime(_Symbol, _Period, 0);
        
        // First bar initialization
        if (node_1772804484172_lastBarTime == 0) {
            node_1772804484172_prevValue1 = node_1772804484172_value1;
            node_1772804484172_prevValue2 = node_1772804484172_value2;
            node_1772804484172_lastTickValue1 = node_1772804484172_value1;
            node_1772804484172_lastTickValue2 = node_1772804484172_value2;
            node_1772804484172_lastBarTime = node_1772804484172_currentBarTime;
            LogInfo("Crossunder node_1772804484172 initialized");
        }
        else {
            // CRITICAL FIX: On new bar, use the LAST TICK value from previous bar
            if (g_NewBar && node_1772804484172_currentBarTime != node_1772804484172_lastBarTime) {
                // lastTickValue contains the close of previous bar (last tick before g_NewBar)
                node_1772804484172_prevValue1 = node_1772804484172_lastTickValue1;
                node_1772804484172_prevValue2 = node_1772804484172_lastTickValue2;
                node_1772804484172_lastBarTime = node_1772804484172_currentBarTime;
                LogDebug("Crossunder node_1772804484172: New bar - prev1=" + DoubleToString(node_1772804484172_prevValue1, 5) + " prev2=" + DoubleToString(node_1772804484172_prevValue2, 5));
            }
            
            // Detect crossunder: curr1 < curr2 AND prev1 >= prev2
            node_1772804484172_result = (node_1772804484172_value1 < node_1772804484172_value2) && (node_1772804484172_prevValue1 >= node_1772804484172_prevValue2);
            
            if (node_1772804484172_result) {
                LogInfo("CROSSUNDER node_1772804484172 TRIGGERED! curr1=" + DoubleToString(node_1772804484172_value1, 5) + " < curr2=" + DoubleToString(node_1772804484172_value2, 5));
            }
        }
        
        // ALWAYS update lastTickValue at end of every tick
        node_1772804484172_lastTickValue1 = node_1772804484172_value1;
        node_1772804484172_lastTickValue2 = node_1772804484172_value2;
        
        // Confirmation bars check (runtime)
        static int node_1772804484172_confirmCount = 0;
        if (inp_crossund_confirmationBar_2804484172 > 0) {
            if (g_NewBar) {
                if (node_1772804484172_result) {
                    node_1772804484172_confirmCount++;
                } else {
                    node_1772804484172_confirmCount = 0;
                }
            }
            node_1772804484172_result = (node_1772804484172_confirmCount >= inp_crossund_confirmationBar_2804484172);
        }


    // Node: logic.and (ID: node_1772732124744)

        // AND Logic (MQL5) - 2 conditions
        bool node_1772732124744_result = ((node_1772804484172_result) && (node_1772732099294_result));

    // Node: logic.threshold (ID: node_1772665118768)

        // Threshold Logic (MQL5)
        double node_1772665118768_value = node_1772662985797_value;
        bool node_1772665118768_result = (node_1772665118768_value < inp_threshol_threshold_2665118768);

    // Node: logic.and (ID: node_1772665216399)

        // AND Logic (MQL5) - 2 conditions
        bool node_1772665216399_result = ((node_1772665233500_result) && (node_1772665118768_result));

    // Node: logic.or (ID: node_1772665357497)

        // OR Logic (MQL5) - 5 conditions
        bool node_1772665357497_result = ((node_1772732312742_result) || (node_1772732322838_result) || (node_1772732162308_result) || (node_1772732124744_result) || (node_1772665216399_result));

    // Node: logic.orderCount (ID: node_1772731653721)

        // Order Count (MQL5)
        int node_1772731653721_count = GetOrderCount("SELL", true, inp_orderCou_magicNumber_2731653721);

    // Node: logic.threshold (ID: node_1772731698324)

        // Threshold Logic (MQL5)
        double node_1772731698324_value = node_1772731653721_count;
        bool node_1772731698324_result = (node_1772731698324_value > inp_threshol_threshold_2731698324);

    // Node: logic.and (ID: node_1772731718684)

        // AND Logic (MQL5) - 2 conditions
        bool node_1772731718684_result = ((node_1772665357497_result) && (node_1772731698324_result));

    // Node: action.closeSell (ID: node_1772665092767)

        // Close Sell Orders (MQL5) - Executes on EVERY TICK for HFT compatibility
        if (node_1772731718684_result) {
            static datetime lastCloseSellTime = 0;
            datetime currentTime = TimeCurrent();
            
            if (currentTime != lastCloseSellTime) {
                int closedCount = 0;
                for (int i = PositionsTotal() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                    ulong ticket = PositionGetTicket(i);
                    if (ticket <= 0) continue;
                    
                    if (PositionGetString(POSITION_SYMBOL) != _Symbol) continue;
                    // Magic Number = 0: Apply to ALL positions of this symbol
                    if (inp_closeSel_magicNumber_2665092767 != 0 && PositionGetInteger(POSITION_MAGIC) != inp_closeSel_magicNumber_2665092767) continue;
                    if (PositionGetInteger(POSITION_TYPE) != POSITION_TYPE_SELL) continue;
                    
                    double profitPips = GetPositionProfitPips(ticket);
                    // Si minProfit <= 0, cerrar TODAS sin filtro de profit
                    if (inp_closeSel_minProfit_2665092767 <= 0 || profitPips >= inp_closeSel_minProfit_2665092767) {
                        if (ClosePosition(ticket)) closedCount++;
                    }
                }
                if (closedCount > 0) {
                    LogInfo("Closed " + IntegerToString(closedCount) + " SELL positions");
                    lastCloseSellTime = currentTime;
                }
            }
        }

}

// ===== DEINITIALIZATION =====

void OnDeinit(const int reason) {
    LogInfo("EA Deinitialized. Reason: " + IntegerToString(reason));

    // Clean up any remaining chart objects
    ObjectsDeleteAll(0);
    
    // Log deinit reason for debugging
    string reasonText = "";
    switch(reason) {
        case REASON_PROGRAM: reasonText = "Expert removed"; break;
        case REASON_REMOVE: reasonText = "Program removed"; break;
        case REASON_RECOMPILE: reasonText = "Recompiled"; break;
        case REASON_CHARTCHANGE: reasonText = "Symbol/timeframe changed"; break;
        case REASON_CHARTCLOSE: reasonText = "Chart closed"; break;
        case REASON_PARAMETERS: reasonText = "Parameters changed"; break;
        case REASON_ACCOUNT: reasonText = "Account changed"; break;
        default: reasonText = "Unknown reason"; break;
    }
    Print("Deinit: ", reasonText);
}

// ===== TESTER FUNCTION - COMPOSITE OPTIMIZATION CRITERION =====
// Uses Custom max in Strategy Tester for best results.
// Penalizes passes with fewer trades than MinimumTrades.
double OnTester() {
    double netProfit    = TesterStatistics(STAT_PROFIT);
    double maxDD        = TesterStatistics(STAT_EQUITY_DD_RELATIVE);
    double totalTrades  = TesterStatistics(STAT_TRADES);
    double winTrades    = TesterStatistics(STAT_PROFIT_TRADES);
    double profitFactor = TesterStatistics(STAT_PROFIT_FACTOR);
    double sharpeRatio  = TesterStatistics(STAT_SHARPE_RATIO);
    double winRate      = (totalTrades > 0) ? (winTrades / totalTrades) * 100.0 : 0;
    double balance      = AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_BALANCE);
    double recoveryFactor = (maxDD > 0.01 && balance > 0)
        ? MathAbs(netProfit) / (maxDD / 100.0 * balance)
        : netProfit;

    // Reject passes with too few trades (returns large negative so they rank last)
    if (totalTrades < MinimumTrades) {
        Print("[OPT] REJECTED: ", (int)totalTrades, " trades < MinimumTrades(", MinimumTrades, ")");
        return -1000.0 + totalTrades;
    }

    // Composite score: balances profitability, consistency, risk and sample size
    double score = 0;
    score += MathMin(profitFactor, 5.0) * 0.30;        // Cap PF at 5 to avoid outliers
    score += MathMax(sharpeRatio, -2.0) * 0.25;         // Sharpe (floor at -2)
    score += (winRate / 100.0) * 0.15;                   // Win rate normalized 0-1
    score += MathMin(recoveryFactor, 10.0) * 0.20;      // Recovery Factor capped at 10
    score += MathLog(MathMax(totalTrades, 1.0)) * 0.10;  // Reward more trades (log scale)

    if (netProfit < 0) score *= 0.5;

    Print("========================================================");
    Print("  OPTIMIZATION PASS RESULTS");
    Print("========================================================");
    Print("Net Profit: ", DoubleToString(netProfit, 2));
    Print("Trades: ", (int)totalTrades, " | Win Rate: ", DoubleToString(winRate, 1), "%");
    Print("Profit Factor: ", DoubleToString(profitFactor, 2),
          " | Sharpe: ", DoubleToString(sharpeRatio, 2));
    Print("Max DD: ", DoubleToString(maxDD, 1), "%",
          " | Recovery: ", DoubleToString(recoveryFactor, 2));
    Print("Composite Score: ", DoubleToString(score, 4));
    if (g_IsBacktestTraining) {
        Print("AI Training Ticks: ", g_BacktestTrainingTicks);
        Print("NEXT: Load trained model in demo/live with same Magic Number");
    }
    Print("========================================================");

    return score;
}


// ===== OPTIMIZATION PHASE CONTROLLER =====
// Automatically configures which parameters to optimize based on OptimizationPhase input.
// Set OptimizationPhase=1 and run optimization, then set best values and run Phase 2, etc.
// Phase 0 = Manual (configure everything yourself in MT5 Inputs tab)
// WORKFLOW: Phase 1 -> set best -> Phase 2 -> set best -> Phase 3 -> set best -> Phase 4

void OnTesterInit() {
    int phase = OptimizationPhase;
    if (phase < 0 || phase > 4) phase = 0;

    if (phase == 0) {
        Print("========================================================");
        Print("  OPTIMIZATION MODE: Manual (Phase 0)");
        Print("  You must configure parameters manually in Inputs tab.");
        Print("  ");
        Print("  >>> To use GUIDED optimization: <<<");
        Print("  1. Set OptimizationPhase = 1 in Inputs");
        Print("  2. Run optimization (Criterion: Custom max)");
        Print("  3. Apply best result, set Phase = 2, repeat");
        Print("========================================================");
        return;
    }

    string phaseNames[] = {"Manual", "Indicators (periods, deviations)", "Logic (thresholds, levels)", "Risk Management (SL/TP, lots)", "Fine-Tuning (filters, AI)"};
    Print("========================================================");
    Print("  GUIDED OPTIMIZATION - Phase ", phase, "/4");
    Print("  Optimizing: ", phaseNames[phase]);
    Print("  MinimumTrades filter: ", MinimumTrades);
    Print("  ");
    Print("  Parameters in each phase:");
    Print("  Phase 1: INDICATORS (periods, deviations) - 61 params");
    Print("  Phase 2: LOGIC (thresholds, confirmations, levels) - 70 params");
    Print("  Phase 3: RISK MANAGEMENT (SL/TP, lots, limits) - 4 params");
    Print("  Phase 4: FINE-TUNING (MA types, filters, AI params) - 33 params");

    Print("  ");
    Print("  Workflow: Phase 1 -> apply best -> Phase 2 -> ...");
    Print("========================================================");

    ParameterSetRange("OptimizationPhase", false, (long)phase, (long)0, (long)1, (long)4);
    ParameterSetRange("MinimumTrades", false, (long)MinimumTrades, (long)10, (long)10, (long)500);
    // Global fixed params: NEVER optimize Magic Number, MaxSpread, EnableTrading (no strategy sense)
    ParameterSetRange("g_MagicNumber", false, (long)g_MagicNumber, (long)g_MagicNumber, (long)0, (long)g_MagicNumber);
    ParameterSetRange("g_MaxSpreadPoints", false, (double)g_MaxSpreadPoints, (double)g_MaxSpreadPoints, (double)0, (double)g_MaxSpreadPoints);
    ParameterSetRange("g_EnableTrading", false, (long)g_EnableTrading, (long)g_EnableTrading, (long)0, (long)g_EnableTrading);

        if (phase == 1)
            ParameterSetRange("inp_hurst_df_period_1288439472", true, (long)inp_hurst_df_period_1288439472, (long)100, (long)90, (long)560);
        else
            ParameterSetRange("inp_hurst_df_period_1288439472", false, (long)inp_hurst_df_period_1288439472, (long)100, (long)90, (long)1000);
        if (phase == 1)
            ParameterSetRange("inp_hurst_df_minLag_1288439472", true, (long)inp_hurst_df_minLag_1288439472, (long)4, (long)2, (long)14);

        else
            ParameterSetRange("inp_hurst_df_trendThreshold_1288439472", false, (double)inp_hurst_df_trendThreshold_1288439472, (double)0.5, (double)0.01, (double)0.9);
        if (phase == 1)
            ParameterSetRange("inp_hurst_df_randomUpperThre_1288439472", true, (double)inp_hurst_df_randomUpperThre_1288439472, (double)0.45, (double)0.01, (double)0.61);
